### [1] [Complexity of an inexact stochastic SQP algorithm for equality constrained optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14351)
*Michael J. O'Neill,Aoji Tang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于随机目标函数和确定性等式约束优化问题的两步长随机SQP算法，建立了不同约束条件下的最坏情况复杂度界限，验证了Byrd-Omojukun步分解策略的理论有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对具有随机目标函数和确定性等式约束的非线性优化问题，现有方法在理论复杂度分析方面存在不足，特别是对于流行的Byrd-Ojomukun步分解策略缺乏严格的理论保证。

Method: 提出了一种不精确的两步长随机序列二次规划算法，采用步分解策略，通过为搜索方向的不同分量分配不同的步长来处理随机梯度估计。

Result: 在无约束条件假设下获得了O(ε_c^{-2})的最坏情况复杂度，在LICQ条件下获得O(ε_c^{-1})复杂度，无论约束条件如何都能达到O(ε_L^{-4})的拉格朗日梯度最优复杂度，数值实验显示算法在不可行性收敛性能上优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 该研究首次为Byrd-Omojukun步分解策略提供了复杂度保证，验证了其理论有效性，提出的算法在不可行性收敛性能上优于现有最先进的随机SQP方法。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider nonlinear optimization problems with a stochastic objective function and deterministic equality constraints. We propose an inexact two-stepsize stochastic sequential quadratic programming (SQP) algorithm and analyze its worst-case complexity under mild assumptions. The method utilizes a step decomposition strategy and handles stochastic gradient estimates by assigning different stepsizes to different components of the search direction. We establish the first known $\mathcal{O}(ε_c^{-2})$ worst-case complexity with respect to the infeasibility measure when no constraint qualification is assumed and a worst-case complexity of $\mathcal{O}(ε_c^{-1})$ when LICQ holds, matching the best known result in the literature. In addition, under mild conditions, our method achieves the optimal $\mathcal{O}(ε_L^{-4})$ complexity with respect to the gradient of the Lagrangian regardless of constraint qualifications. Our results provide the first complexity guarantees for the popular Byrd-Omojukun step decomposition strategy and verify its theoretical efficacy. Numerical experiments show that our algorithm has a superior infeasibility convergence performance and a competitive KKT convergence rate compared to the state-of-the-art stochastic SQP method.

</details>


### [2] [A Noise Tolerant SQP Algorithm for Inequality Constrained Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14368)
*Figen Oztoprak,Richard Byrd*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对含噪声函数和导数评估的约束优化问题的SQP算法，该算法能够处理目标函数和约束中的有界噪声，并通过线搜索和松弛技术实现全局收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界优化问题中经常存在测量噪声，传统优化算法对噪声敏感。需要开发能够处理目标函数和约束评估中都含有有界噪声的鲁棒优化算法。

Method: 采用序列二次规划(SQP)框架，结合线搜索方法和松弛技术处理噪声。使用噪声感知的拟牛顿更新，算法能够适应目标函数和约束评估中的有界噪声。

Result: 理论分析表明算法具有全局收敛性，数值实验验证算法能够达到与噪声水平和问题相关参数成正比的精度，符合理论预期。

Conclusion: 提出的噪声鲁棒SQP算法能够有效处理约束优化问题中的有界噪声，在理论和数值上都表现出良好的性能，为含噪声优化问题提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: We propose a sequential quadratic programming (SQP) algorithm for inequality constrained optimization that is robust to the presence of bounded noise in function and derivative evaluations. We cover the case where constraint evaluations contain noise as well as the objective. The proposed algorithm is a line search SQP method with relaxations to deal with noise. We study the effect of noise on the global convergence behavior of the algorithm. We implement the algorithm with noise-aware quasi-Newton updates, and numerically observe that the algorithm can achieve accuracy proportional to the noise level and problem-dependent parameters, as suggested by the theory.

</details>


### [3] [Empirical Evaluation of Policy-Based Reinforcement Learning for Dynamic Service Control in an M/M/1 Queue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14406)
*Joseph Walton,Gabriel Nicolosi*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 研究比较了三种基于策略的强化学习算法（REINFORCE、A2C、PPO）在M/M/1队列服务率控制问题中的性能，使用两种状态表示方法，评估收敛速度、采样效率、策略质量和伪遗憾等指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然强化学习在随机控制中应用日益增多，但很少有研究系统性地检验基于策略的方法在半马尔可夫决策过程（SMDP）建模的排队环境中的表现。本研究旨在填补这一空白，探究基于策略的强化学习算法在M/M/1队列服务率控制问题中的性能。

Method: 将M/M/1队列服务率控制问题建模为SMDP，决策点发生在每次新服务开始时，智能体可以从有限的速度集合中选择不同的服务率。研究比较了三种基于策略的强化学习算法：REINFORCE、Actor-Critic（A2C）和Proximal Policy Optimization（PPO）。在模拟环境中训练时使用了两种状态表示：瞬时队列长度和包含一步队列历史的增强状态。目标函数旨在管理系统拥塞和能源成本。

Result: 性能评估基于收敛速度、采样效率、策略质量和相对于稳态最优解的伪遗憾等指标。具体结果未在摘要中详细说明，但研究对这些算法在排队控制问题中的表现进行了系统比较。

Conclusion: 该研究为基于策略的强化学习算法在半马尔可夫决策过程建模的排队控制问题中的应用提供了系统性评估，有助于理解不同算法在服务率控制问题中的相对优势和局限性，为实际系统优化提供参考。

Abstract: While reinforcement learning has been increasingly applied to stochastic control, few studies have systematically examined policy-based methods in queuing environments modeled as a semi-Markov decision process (SMDP). To address this gap, we investigate how policy-based reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms perform when applied to the control of service rates in an M/M/1 queue, a common queuing model for manufacturing, computing, and service systems. The problem is formulated as an SMDP in which decisions occur at each new service, allowing an agent to select different service rates from a finite set of speeds, aiming to minimize an objective function that manages system congestion and energy costs. Three policy-based reinforcement learning algorithms, namely REINFORCE, Actor-Critic (A2C), and Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), are trained in a simulated environment using two state representations: the instantaneous queue length and an augmented state that includes a one-step queue history. Performance is evaluated in terms of convergence speed, sampling efficiency, policy quality, and pseudo-regret relative to the steady-state optimum.

</details>


### [4] [PANOC-lite: A simpler and more efficient algorithm for composite minimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14503)
*Alexander Bodard,Pieter Pas,Andreas Themelis,Panagiotis Patrinos*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出一种用于复合优化的简单高效线搜索方法，通过快速牛顿型方向加速近端梯度迭代，仅需标准近端梯度算子，具有更便宜的回溯过程和更大的步长范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有复合优化方法如PANOC和ZeroFPR需要额外的梯度计算，回溯过程成本较高，步长范围有限。本文旨在开发一种更简单高效的方法，减少计算开销，扩大步长选择范围，同时保持收敛性能。

Method: 提出基于简单操作的线搜索方法，仅需标准近端梯度算子（假设非光滑项凸）。关键改进包括：1）更便宜的回溯过程，无需额外梯度计算；2）扩大允许步长范围；3）使用新型评价函数，比前向后向包络等替代方案计算成本更低。

Result: 在常规假设下建立了全局子序列收敛和局部超线性收敛。在具有碰撞避免约束的模型预测控制问题以及LIBSVM和CUTEst基准测试上验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种简单高效的复合优化算法，具有计算优势（无需额外梯度评估的回溯过程）和理论保证（全局和局部收敛性），在多个实际问题上表现出良好性能。

Abstract: This work introduces a simple and efficient linesearch method for composite minimization that accelerates proximal-gradient iterations with fast Newton-type directions. Our algorithm is based on simple operations and only requires the standard proximal-gradient oracle, similar to PANOC and ZeroFPR, provided that the nonsmooth term is convex. Noteworthy improvements include a cheaper backtracking procedure, in the sense that no additional gradients need to be evaluated, and an enlarged range of permitted stepsizes. Global subsequential convergence and local superlinear convergence are established under conventional assumptions by considering a novel merit function which is less expensive to evaluate than alternatives like the forward-backward envelope. Finally, the proposed approach is validated on model predictive control problems with collision avoidance constraints, as well as on the LIBSVM and CUTEst benchmarks.

</details>


### [5] [Anderson Acceleration for Linearly Converging SQP-Type Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14803)
*Jonathan Frey,David Kiessling,Katrin Baumgärtner,Moritz Diehl*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文研究了将Anderson加速应用于约束优化中的SQP方法，通过在acados框架中实现并测试最优控制问题，证明了该方法能显著改善收敛性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Anderson加速在加速定点迭代方面效果显著，但很少应用于约束优化特别是序列二次规划方法。作者希望探索如何将AA技术应用于SQP方法以改善其局部收敛行为。

Method: 提出将Anderson加速应用于一般族（不精确）SQP型方法，并引入简单启发式策略来缓解远离解时收敛速度较慢的问题。该方法在acados软件框架中实现，并通过最优控制数值算例进行验证。

Result: 数值实验表明，不同SQP型方法在收敛性方面均获得了一致的改进，证明了Anderson加速对SQP方法的有效性。

Conclusion: Anderson加速可以成功应用于约束优化中的SQP方法，显著改善局部收敛行为，特别是在最优控制问题中表现出良好的性能提升。

Abstract: Although Anderson acceleration (AA) is known to speed up fixed-point iterations, it is rarely applied in constrained optimization, in particular sequential quadratic programming (SQP). We show that the local convergence behavior of a general family of (inexact) SQP-type methods can benefit from AA and introduce a simple heuristic to alleviate slower convergence farther from the solution. The method is implemented in the software framework acados. Numerical examples from optimal control illustrate consistent improvements in convergence of different SQP-type methods.

</details>


### [6] [Towards Optimal Passive Feedback Control of LTI Systems under LQR Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14854)
*Armin Gießler,Pol Jané-Soneira,Sören Hohmann*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文研究连续时间LTI系统的状态反馈设计，目标是在使闭环系统相对于外部端口严格无源的同时，最小化无扰动情况下的标准LQR成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于需要为具有控制输入和外部输入输出对的连续时间LTI系统设计状态反馈控制器。传统LQR方法虽然能最小化二次成本，但无法保证系统的无源性特性。无源性在控制系统设计中具有重要意义，特别是在鲁棒性、稳定性和能量管理方面。然而，同时满足无源性约束和LQR最优性导致了一个包含双线性矩阵不等式(BMI)的难以处理的优化问题。

Method: 论文采用间接方法：首先分析无源化反馈增益集合的性质，发现该集合是无界的、可能非凸的、路径连通的且可收缩的。然后，通过一个紧致凸多面体来内近似这个无源化增益集合。最后，采用投影梯度流算法在该凸多面体内计算最小化LQR成本的增益。这种方法将原本难以处理的BMI约束问题转化为在凸集上的优化问题。

Result: 理论分析表明无源化反馈增益集合具有特定的拓扑性质（无界、可能非凸、路径连通、可收缩）。提出的间接方法通过凸多面体内近似和投影梯度流，能够有效计算满足无源性约束的LQR最优增益。数值示例验证了该方法的有效性，展示了其在同时保证系统无源性和性能优化方面的能力。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种解决LTI系统同时满足无源性约束和LQR最优性这一挑战性问题的有效方法。通过分析无源化增益集合的拓扑性质，并采用凸内近似和投影梯度流技术，成功将原本难以处理的BMI约束优化问题转化为可计算的凸优化问题。该方法为控制系统设计提供了新的工具，特别适用于需要同时考虑性能和无源性的应用场景。

Abstract: We study state-feedback design for continuous-time LTI systems with a control input and an external input-output pair. Our objective is to determine feedback gains that render the closed-loop system (strictly) passive with respect to the external port while minimizing the standard LQR cost in the disturbance-free case. The resulting constrained optimization problem is intractable due to bilinear matrix inequalities. We analyze the set of passivating gains, showing it is unbounded, possibly nonconvex, path-connected, and contractible. We propose an indirect approach, in which the set of passivating feedback gains is inner-approximated by a compact, convex polytope. A projected gradient flow is employed to compute a gain within this polytope that minimizes the LQR cost. Numerical examples illustrate the effectiveness of the method.

</details>


### [7] [Affine-coupled Distributed Optimization via Distributed Proximal Jacobian ADMM with Quantized Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14861)
*Xu Du,Boyu Han,Ivano Notarnicola,Karl H. Johansson,Apostolos I. Rikos*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出一种结合量化共识的分布式PJ-ADMM算法，用于有向图上的资源分配优化，在有限通信带宽下实现高效分布式求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决有向通信图环境下，节点间通信带宽受限时的分布式资源分配优化问题。现有方法通常假设无限制通信或需要高精度信息交换，难以在实际带宽受限场景中应用。

Method: 将中心化PJ-ADMM与有限级量化共识方案相结合，设计分布式算法。通过量化机制压缩节点间交换的信息，在保证收敛性的同时显著降低通信开销。

Result: 在凸目标函数假设下，算法实现次线性收敛到最优解邻域，收敛精度由量化级别明确界定。数值实验表明，相比现有方法，该算法在保持竞争性能的同时具有更高的通信效率。

Conclusion: 所提算法为有向图环境下带宽受限的分布式优化问题提供了有效解决方案，通过量化机制平衡了收敛精度与通信开销，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: This paper investigates distributed resource allocation optimization over directed graphs with limited communication bandwidth. We develop a novel distributed algorithm that integrates the centralized Proximal Jacobian Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (PJ-ADMM) with a finite-level quantized consensus scheme, enabling nodes to cooperatively solve the optimization in a distributed fashion. Under the assumption of convex objective functions, we establish that the proposed algorithm achieves sublinear convergence to a neighborhood of the optimal solution, with the convergence accuracy explicitly bounded by the quantization level. Numerical experiments validate that the algorithm achieves competitive performance compared to existing approaches while exhibiting communication efficiency.

</details>


### [8] [Mix-CALADIN: A Distributed Algorithm for Consensus Mixed-Integer Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14897)
*Boyu Han,Xu Du,Karl H. Johansson,Apostolos I. Rikos*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出了一种处理混合整数（特别是布尔变量）分布式共识优化问题的新算法，扩展CALADIN框架，无需局部混合整数求解器，在凸和非凸问题上均提供收敛保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决分布式共识优化问题中混合整数变量的挑战，特别是布尔变量。现有方法通常依赖局部混合整数求解器，需要开发无需此类求解器的新方法。

Method: 扩展CALADIN框架，引入专门处理布尔变量的技术，无需局部混合整数求解器。在目标函数满足Lipschitz连续性的温和假设下，为凸和非凸混合整数规划问题建立收敛保证。

Result: 数值实验表明，该算法在性能上与现有方法相当，同时提供严格的收敛保证，适用于凸和非凸混合整数规划问题。

Conclusion: 提出了一种处理混合整数（特别是布尔变量）分布式共识优化问题的有效算法，无需局部混合整数求解器，在凸和非凸问题上均具有收敛保证，性能与现有方法相当。

Abstract: This paper addresses distributed consensus optimization problems with mixed-integer variables, with a specific focus on Boolean variables. We introduce a novel distributed algorithm that extends the Consensus Augmented Lagrangian Alternating Direction Inexact Newton (CALADIN) framework by incorporating specialized techniques for handling Boolean variables without relying on local mixed-integer solvers. Under the mild assumption of Lipschitz continuity of the objective functions, we establish rigorous convergence guarantees for both convex and nonconvex mixed-integer programming problems. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the proposed algorithm achieves competitive performance compared to existing approaches while providing rigorous convergence guarantees.

</details>


### [9] [Dynamic Lagrange Multipliers in a Non-concave Utility Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14924)
*Yang Liu,Alexander Schied,Zhenyu Shen*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出"动态拉格朗日乘子"方法，在非凹效用函数框架下连接鞅对偶方法和动态规划方法，证明拉格朗日乘子函数等于价值函数关于财富的偏导数，并展示其经济解释为包络定理的动态影子价格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在连续时间投资组合选择中，非凹效用函数场景下，鞅对偶方法在完全市场中广泛应用，而动态规划方法有时会导致HJB方程的奇异解。需要建立两种方法之间的联系，提供更统一的理论框架。

Method: 提出"动态拉格朗日乘子"概念，在非凹效用函数框架下，证明拉格朗日乘子函数（鞅对偶方法）等于与价值函数相关的共轭对偶点（动态规划方法），即价值函数关于财富的偏导数。通过最优财富和定价核过程展示动态乘子过程的齐次性。

Result: 成功连接了鞅对偶和动态规划两种方法，证明拉格朗日乘子函数等于价值函数的财富偏导数。动态乘子过程通过最优财富和定价核过程表现出齐次性，为包络定理提供了动态影子价格的经济解释。通过非凹效用例子恢复了经典最优结果并进行了数值验证。

Conclusion: 动态拉格朗日乘子方法为连续时间非凹效用投资组合选择提供了统一框架，成功连接了鞅对偶和动态规划两种主流方法，揭示了拉格朗日乘子的经济意义，并通过数值验证证明了方法的有效性。

Abstract: In continuous-time portfolio selection for non-concave utility functions, the martingale duality approach is widely adopted in complete markets, while the dynamic programming approach may sometimes lead to singular solutions of the Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman (HJB) equation. We propose "dynamic Lagrange multipliers" in a non-concave utility framework, bridging two approaches and demonstrating that the Lagrangian multiplier function (in the martingale duality approach) equals the conjugate dual point related to the value function (in dynamic programming), which is exactly its partial derivative with respect to wealth. Moreover, the dynamic multiplier process exhibits homogeneity via the optimal wealth and pricing kernel processes, offering intuitive economic interpretations as a dynamic shadow price of the envelope theorem. Finally, classical optimal results are recovered and numerically validated by non-concave utility examples.

</details>


### [10] [A pointwise tracking optimal control problem for a fractional, semilinear PDE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14940)
*Enrique Otarola,Abner J. Salgado*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 研究带有点值跟踪的分数阶半线性椭圆PDE最优控制问题，扩散由谱分数阶拉普拉斯算子(-Δ)^s描述(s∈(1/2,1))，处理伴随方程具有Dirac测度奇异右端项的非凸控制问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究分数阶半线性椭圆PDE的最优控制问题，特别关注点值跟踪控制。主要挑战在于伴随方程具有Dirac测度奇异右端项，且控制问题本身是非凸的，需要建立完整的优化理论框架。

Method: 采用谱分数阶拉普拉斯算子(-Δ)^s(s∈(1/2,1))保证状态的点值评估适定性。建立最优解存在性，推导一阶最优性条件，以及必要和充分的二阶最优性条件，处理伴随方程的奇异右端项。

Result: 证明了最优解的存在性，推导了一阶最优性条件，建立了必要和充分的二阶最优性条件，为分数阶半线性椭圆PDE的点值跟踪控制问题提供了完整的优化理论框架。

Conclusion: 成功解决了具有点值跟踪的分数阶半线性椭圆PDE最优控制问题，克服了伴随方程奇异右端项和非凸性的困难，建立了完整的优化理论，为这类问题的数值实现提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We analyze an optimal control problem with pointwise tracking for a fractional semilinear elliptic partial differential equation. The diffusion is characterized by the spectral fractional Laplacian $(-Δ)^s$ with $s \in (1/2,1)$, a range that guarantees the well-posedness of point evaluations of the state. In addition to the nonconvexity of the control problem, the main difficulty is that the adjoint equation is a fractional partial differential equation with a singular right-hand side: a linear combination of Dirac measures. We establish the existence of optimal solutions and derive first-order as well as necessary and sufficient second-order optimality conditions.

</details>


### [11] [Duality attainment and strict feasibility of the generalized moment problem and its relaxations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15072)
*Sami Halaseh,Victor Magron,Mateusz Skomra*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文研究具有多项式矩约束的广义矩问题，在紧致基本半代数集上分析对偶问题的可达性和平方和层次结构的收敛性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义矩问题在多项式矩约束下，虽然平方和层次结构提供收敛界，但对偶问题的可达性和层次结构中每个有限维强化的可达性尚未得到充分研究，特别是在支持集具有特定代数结构时

Method: 研究紧致基本半代数集上的广义矩问题：1) 当X有非空内部时；2) 当X是形成Gröbner基且生成实根理想的指定多项式的零点集时。在相对内部假设下，证明无限维对偶问题的可达性，以及每个有限维平方和强化的可达性。提供两种证明方法：一是通过调整二次模的闭性结果，二是基于Csiszár的指数密度构造寻找严格可行测度

Result: 在相对内部假设下，证明了无限维对偶问题的可达性，以及每个有限维平方和强化的可达性。特别讨论了X为球面乘积的特殊情况，并将结果应用于张量优化和量子信息论中的广义矩问题实例

Conclusion: 该研究为具有多项式矩约束的广义矩问题提供了可达性理论框架，特别是在支持集具有特定代数结构时。两种不同的证明方法增强了结果的可靠性，对张量优化和量子信息论等领域的应用具有重要意义

Abstract: The generalized moment problem (GMP) is an infinite dimensional linear problem over the cone of finite nonnegative Borel measures. When a GMP instance involves finitely many polynomial moment constraints, moment/sum-of-squares hierarchies provide a sequence of bounds converging to the optimal value. We consider GMP instances with measures supported over a compact basic semialgebraic set $X$. We study the case when $X$ has nonempty interior, and the case when $X$ is the vanishing set of prescribed polynomials forming a Gröbner basis of the ideal they generate, which we assume is real radical. Under a relative interior assumption, we show attainment of the infinite dimensional dual problem, and attainment of each associated finite dimensional sum-of-squares strengthening. For the latter we present two disjoint proofs. The first is obtained by adapting results regarding the closedness of quadratic modules, and the second builds on Csiszár's work on exponential density constructions to find a strictly feasible measure. Finally, we discuss the special case where $X$ is the product of spheres, and applications of our results to GMP instances arising from tensor optimization and quantum information theory.

</details>


### [12] [A Robust Optimization Approach for Scheduling with Uncertain Start-Time Dependent Costs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15161)
*Sofía Rodríguez-Ballesteros,Javier Alcaraz,Laura Anton-Sanchez,Marc Goerigk,Dorothee Henke*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实调度场景中成本随时间波动（如能源价格、劳动力成本），且存在不确定性，需要鲁棒优化方法来应对这种波动

Method: 采用两阶段鲁棒优化：第一阶段决定活动执行顺序；第二阶段在成本场景揭示后确定各活动开始时间。针对连续和离散预算不确定性开发模型和求解方法

Result: 证明该问题是NP难且不可近似，其鲁棒对应问题同样复杂；评估第一阶段解在离散不确定性下也是NP难的。通过计算实验比较不同方法，展示提前考虑不确定性的优势

Conclusion: 该研究为处理具有开始时间相关成本且存在不确定性的调度问题提供了鲁棒优化框架，证明了问题的计算复杂性，并开发了有效的求解方法

Abstract: In this work, we study a single-machine scheduling problem that aims at minimizing the total cost of a schedule subject to start-time dependent costs. This framework naturally captures scenarios where costs fluctuate throughout the day, such as time-varying energy or labor prices. To model more realistic scenarios, we assume that these costs lie within a budgeted uncertainty set and propose a two-stage robust optimization approach. In a first stage, the order in which activities should be executed is decided. After a cost scenario has been revealed, the starting times for each activity are established, subject to the ordering from the first stage. We demonstrate that the proposed problem is NP-hard and not approximable, implying the complexity of its robust counterpart. Furthermore, we show that already evaluating a first-stage solution is NP-hard when the uncertainty set is discrete. We develop models and solution methods for both continuous and discrete budgeted uncertainty. In computational experiments, we compare these approaches and demonstrate the advantages of including uncertainty beforehand.

Furthermore, to decrease computational complexity, we design an event-triggered update strategy that avoids updating Hessian and Jacobian matrices at every iteration. The proposed method achieves local convergence and enhanced communication efficiency, making it well suited for time-critical applications. Numerical experiments demonstrate that our approach achieves competitive performance while exhibiting superior computational efficiency in real-time scenarios, validating its practical applicability for time-sensitive distributed optimization challenges.

### [14] [Pricing Electric Vehicle Charging and Station Access via Copositive Duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15227)
*Nanfei Jiang,Yi Zhou,Josh A. Taylor,Mahnoosh Alizadeh*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文提出首个考虑二进制充电站接入约束的边际定价机制，通过完全正规划(CPP)和余正规划(COP)解决EV充电的混合整数线性规划问题，实现激励相容的定价方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电动汽车在公共充电站的优化充电涉及连续的能量分配决策和离散的充电站接入决策，形成混合整数线性规划问题。传统的边际定价方法无法处理这种离散性，需要开发新的定价机制来同时考虑充电容量限制和充电设备拥堵效应。

Method: 利用Burer(2009)的结果，将EV充电问题表达为完全正规划(CPP)，其对偶是余正规划(COP)。通过COP对偶变量作为边际价格，构建定价机制。开发了特定问题的内近似和降维技术来提高COP求解的计算可行性。

Result: 提出的定价机制在数学上保证了运营商的收入充足性和每个EV用户的个体理性。数值实验表明，该机制能够捕捉离散拥堵效应，使用户激励与系统最优分配一致，优于分时电价和凸松弛基准方法。

Conclusion: 该研究首次开发了考虑二进制充电站接入约束的边际定价机制，通过COP对偶变量作为有效影子价格，解决了离散非凸优化问题的定价挑战，为EV充电基础设施的激励相容定价提供了理论框架和实用工具。

Abstract: Optimized charging of electric vehicles (EVs) at public locations consists of two decisions: how much energy to deliver at what times, which is continuous, and where to plug in, which is binary. This makes optimizing EV charging a mixed-integer linear program (MILP). This discreteness undermines traditional marginal pricing methods. In this paper, we develop the first marginal-price-based mechanism for pricing EV charging with binary station access constraints. Using the result of Burer (2009), we express the EV charging as a completely positive program (CPP), whose dual is a copositive program (COP). This convex dual admits valid shadow prices even though the original allocation problem is discrete and nonconvex. By interpreting the COP dual variables as marginal prices, we construct a pricing mechanism that captures EV supply equipment (EVSE) congestion as well as charging-capacity limits. We prove that the resulting mechanism is revenue-adequate for the operator and individually rational for every EV user, in the strong sense that each user maximizes their own welfare by accepting their assigned charging plan rather than deviating to any alternative option. We further develop problem-specific inner-approximation and dimension-reduction techniques that substantially improve the computational tractability of solving the COP in our setting. Numerical experiments on both small and large scale charging instances demonstrate that our pricing mechanism captures discrete congestion effects and aligns user incentives with the system-optimal assignment, outperforming time-of-use (TOU) and convex relaxation benchmarks.

</details>

### [15] [The Devil Is in Gradient Entanglement: Energy-Aware Gradient Coordinator for Robust Generalized Category Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14176)
*Haiyang Zheng,Nan Pu,Yaqi Cai,Teng Long,Wenjing Li,Nicu Sebe,Zhun Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出EAGC（能量感知梯度协调器）解决GCD中梯度纠缠问题，通过AGA锚定已知类梯度方向，EEP自适应投影未标记梯度，减少已知类与新颖类表示子空间重叠，提升分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义类别发现（GCD）利用标记数据对已知或未知类别的未标记样本进行分类。现有方法联合优化监督和无监督目标，但存在优化干扰问题。通过定量分析发现梯度纠缠问题：1）扭曲监督梯度，削弱已知类间区分能力；2）导致已知类与新颖类表示子空间重叠，降低新颖类别的可分性。

Method: 提出能量感知梯度协调器（EAGC），包含两个组件：1）基于锚点的梯度对齐（AGA）：引入参考模型锚定标记样本的梯度方向，保护已知类的判别结构免受未标记梯度干扰；2）能量感知弹性投影（EEP）：将未标记梯度软投影到已知类子空间的补空间，基于能量系数自适应缩放投影，根据未标记样本与已知子空间的对齐程度调整，减少子空间重叠而不抑制可能属于已知类的未标记样本。

Result: 实验表明EAGC能持续提升现有方法性能，在多个基准测试中建立了新的最先进结果。该方法作为即插即用的梯度级模块，有效解决了GCD中的优化干扰问题。

Conclusion: EAGC通过显式调节优化过程解决了GCD中的梯度纠缠问题。AGA保护已知类判别结构，EEP自适应处理未标记梯度，共同减少表示子空间重叠。该方法通用性强，能有效提升现有GCD方法的性能。

Abstract: Generalized Category Discovery (GCD) leverages labeled data to categorize unlabeled samples from known or unknown classes. Most previous methods jointly optimize supervised and unsupervised objectives and achieve promising results. However, inherent optimization interference still limits their ability to improve further. Through quantitative analysis, we identify a key issue, i.e., gradient entanglement, which 1) distorts supervised gradients and weakens discrimination among known classes, and 2) induces representation-subspace overlap between known and novel classes, reducing the separability of novel categories. To address this issue, we propose the Energy-Aware Gradient Coordinator (EAGC), a plug-and-play gradient-level module that explicitly regulates the optimization process. EAGC comprises two components: Anchor-based Gradient Alignment (AGA) and Energy-aware Elastic Projection (EEP). AGA introduces a reference model to anchor the gradient directions of labeled samples, preserving the discriminative structure of known classes against the interference of unlabeled gradients. EEP softly projects unlabeled gradients onto the complement of the known-class subspace and derives an energy-based coefficient to adaptively scale the projection for each unlabeled sample according to its degree of alignment with the known subspace, thereby reducing subspace overlap without suppressing unlabeled samples that likely belong to known classes. Experiments show that EAGC consistently boosts existing methods and establishes new state-of-the-art results. Code is available at https://haiyangzheng.github.io/EAGC.

</details>


### [16] [MixAtlas: Uncertainty-aware Data Mixture Optimization for Multimodal LLM Midtraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14198)
*Bingbing Wen,Sirajul Salekin,Feiyang Kang,Bill Howe,Lucy Lu Wang,Javier Movellan,Manjot Bilkhu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态训练方法通常只在单一维度（数据格式或任务类型）上调整数据混合，缺乏系统化的多维度优化方法。领域重加权可以提升样本效率和下游泛化能力，但多模态预训练中的数据混合优化尚未充分探索。

Method: MixAtlas将训练语料库沿两个轴分解：图像概念（通过CLIP嵌入发现的10个视觉领域聚类）和任务监督（5种目标类型包括字幕生成、OCR、定位、检测和VQA）。使用小型代理模型（Qwen2-0.5B）配合高斯过程代理和GP-UCB采集函数，在混合空间中进行搜索，搜索预算与基于回归的基线相同但能找到性能更优的混合。

Result: 在10个涵盖视觉理解、文档推理和多模态推理的基准测试中，优化后的混合在Qwen2-7B上比最强基线平均性能提升8.5%-17.6%；在Qwen2.5-7B上提升1.0%-3.3%。两种设置都能在最多2倍更少的训练步数内达到基线相当的训练损失。在0.5B代理模型上发现的配方可以跨Qwen模型家族迁移到7B规模的训练。

Conclusion: MixAtlas提供了一种系统化的多模态预训练数据混合优化方法，通过双轴分解和高效搜索策略，能够生成可迁移的基准目标数据配方，显著提升模型性能和训练效率。

Abstract: Domain reweighting can improve sample efficiency and downstream generalization, but data-mixture optimization for multimodal midtraining remains largely unexplored. Current multimodal training recipes tune mixtures along a single dimension, typically data format or task type. We introduce MixAtlas, a method that produces benchmark-targeted data recipes that can be inspected, adapted, and transferred to new corpora. MixAtlas decomposes the training corpus along two axes: image concepts (10 visual-domain clusters discovered via CLIP embeddings) and task supervision (5 objective types including captioning, OCR, grounding, detection, and VQA). Using small proxy models (Qwen2-0.5B) paired with a Gaussian-process surrogate and GP-UCB acquisition, MixAtlas searches the resulting mixture space with the same proxy budget as regression-based baselines but finds better-performing mixtures. We evaluate on 10 benchmarks spanning visual understanding, document reasoning, and multimodal reasoning. On Qwen2-7B, optimized mixtures improve average performance by 8.5%-17.6% over the strongest baseline; on Qwen2.5-7B, gains are 1.0%-3.3%. Both settings reach baseline-equivalent training loss in up to 2 times fewer steps. Recipes discovered on 0.5B proxies transfer to 7B-scale training across Qwen model families.

</details>

Abstract: This paper proposes a machine learning assisted portfolio optimization framework designed for low data environments and regime uncertainty. Results show that student models can match or outperform the CVaR teacher in several settings, while achieving improved robustness under regime shifts and reduced turnover. These findings suggest that hybrid optimization learning approaches can enhance portfolio construction in data constrained environments

### [18] [Towards Verified and Targeted Explanations through Formal Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14209)
*Hanchen David Wang,Diego Manzanas Lopez,Preston K. Robinette,Ipek Oguz,Taylor T. Johnson,Meiyi Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ViTaX：首个提供形式化保证的针对性半事实解释框架，专注于安全关键系统中特定高风险误分类的防御验证


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有XAI方法存在缺陷：启发式归因技术（如LIME、积分梯度）缺乏数学保证，而形式化方法虽然验证鲁棒性但非针对性，无法区分不同误分类的风险等级。在安全关键系统中，不同误分类的后果差异巨大（如将"停止"标志误分类为"60 kph"比误分类为"禁止超车"更危险）

Method: 提出ViTaX框架，针对给定输入（类别y）和用户指定的关键替代类别t：1）识别对y->t转换最敏感的最小特征子集；2）应用形式可达性分析，保证在epsilon扰动下这些特征不会导致分类翻转到t。通过"针对性epsilon鲁棒性"形式化验证特征子集在向特定目标类扰动时的鲁棒性

Result: 在MNIST、GTSRB、EMNIST和TaxiNet数据集上的评估显示，ViTaX在最小解释基数下实现了超过30%的保真度提升，是首个提供针对用户指定替代类别的模型弹性形式化保证的解释方法

Conclusion: ViTaX填补了现有XAI方法的空白，为安全关键应用提供了具有数学保证的针对性解释，能够验证模型对特定高风险误分类的防御能力，在解释保真度和针对性方面显著优于现有方法

Abstract: As deep neural networks are deployed in safety-critical domains such as autonomous driving and medical diagnosis, stakeholders need explanations that are interpretable but also trustworthy with formal guarantees. Existing XAI methods fall short: heuristic attribution techniques (e.g., LIME, Integrated Gradients) highlight influential features but offer no mathematical guarantees about decision boundaries, while formal methods verify robustness yet remain untargeted, analyzing the nearest boundary regardless of whether it represents a critical risk. In safety-critical systems, not all misclassifications carry equal consequences; confusing a "Stop" sign for a "60 kph" sign is far more dangerous than confusing it with a "No Passing" sign. We introduce ViTaX (Verified and Targeted Explanations), a formal XAI framework that generates targeted semifactual explanations with mathematical guarantees. For a given input (class y) and a user-specified critical alternative (class t), ViTaX: (1) identifies the minimal feature subset most sensitive to the y->t transition, and (2) applies formal reachability analysis to guarantee that perturbing these features by epsilon cannot flip the classification to t. We formalize this through Targeted epsilon-Robustness, certifying whether a feature subset remains robust under perturbation toward a specific target class. ViTaX is the first method to provide formally guaranteed explanations of a model's resilience against user-identified alternatives. Evaluations on MNIST, GTSRB, EMNIST, and TaxiNet demonstrate over 30% fidelity improvement with minimal explanation cardinality.

</details>


### [19] [Shapley Value-Guided Adaptive Ensemble Learning for Explainable Financial Fraud Detection with U.S. Regulatory Compliance Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14231)
*Mohammad Nasir Uddin,Md Munna Aziz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出SHAP引导自适应集成(SGAE)方法，通过动态调整基于SHAP归因一致性的集成权重，在欺诈检测中实现高AUC-ROC(0.8837/0.9245)，并全面评估了LSTM、Transformer和GNN-GraphSAGE在IEEE-CIS数据集上的性能，满足金融监管合规要求。

Motivation: 金融犯罪每年给美国机构造成超过320亿美元损失。尽管AI欺诈检测工具日益先进，但在实际应用中面临主要障碍：许多模型作为黑箱运行，无法提供OCC Bulletin 2011-12和Federal Reserve SR 11-7等法规要求的透明、可审计的解释。需要开发既准确又可解释的欺诈检测模型以满足监管合规要求。

Method: 1. 全面评估解释质量：包括忠实性(充分性和全面性，k=5,10,15)和稳定性(30个bootstrap样本的Kendall's W)。2. 提出SHAP引导自适应集成(SGAE)：基于SHAP归因一致性动态调整每笔交易的集成权重。3. 完整三架构评估：在590,540笔交易的IEEE-CIS数据集上评估LSTM、Transformer和GNN-GraphSAGE架构。

Result: 1. XGBoost+TreeExplainer实现近乎完美的稳定性(W=0.9912)，LSTM+DeepExplainer表现较弱(W=0.4962)。2. SGAE在所有测试模型中达到最高AUC-ROC(0.8837保留集；0.9245交叉验证)。3. GNN-GraphSAGE表现最佳：AUC-ROC 0.9248，F1=0.6013。所有结果直接映射到OCC、SR 11-7和BSA-AML监管合规要求。

Conclusion: 研究证明了可解释AI在金融欺诈检测中的可行性，SGAE方法通过动态集成权重调整实现了高性能，GNN-GraphSAGE在复杂交易数据上表现优异。工作为金融机构提供了满足监管要求的透明、可审计的欺诈检测解决方案，将模型性能与具体合规要求直接关联。

Abstract: Financial crime costs U.S. institutions over $32 billion each year. Although AI tools for fraud detection have become more advanced, their use in real-world systems still faces a major obstacle: many of these models operate as black boxes that cannot provide the transparent, auditable explanations required by regulations such as OCC Bulletin 2011-12 and Federal Reserve SR 11-7. This study makes three main contributions. First, it offers a thorough evaluation of explanation quality across faithfulness (sufficiency and comprehensiveness at k=5, 10, and 15) and stability (Kendall's W across 30 bootstrap samples). XGBoost paired with TreeExplainer achieves near-perfect stability (W=0.9912), while LSTM with DeepExplainer shows weak results (W=0.4962). Second, the paper introduces the SHAP-Guided Adaptive Ensemble (SGAE), which dynamically adjusts per-transaction ensemble weights based on SHAP attribution agreement, achieving the highest AUC-ROC among all tested models (0.8837 held-out; 0.9245 cross-validation). Third, a complete three-architecture evaluation of LSTM, Transformer, and GNN-GraphSAGE on the full 590,540-transaction IEEE-CIS dataset is provided, with GNN-GraphSAGE achieving AUC-ROC 0.9248 and F1=0.6013. All results are mapped directly to OCC, SR 11-7, and BSA-AML regulatory compliance requirements.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出DPF-GFD模型：1) 对原始图应用beta小波算子捕捉关键结构模式；2) 基于距离的节点表示构建相似图并应用改进的低通滤波器；3) 通过监督表示学习融合两个图的嵌入特征；4) 使用集成树模型评估未标记节点的欺诈风险。

Abstract: Fraud detection on graph data can be viewed as a demanding task that requires distinguishing between different types of nodes. However, fraud graphs inherently exhibit relation camouflage, high heterophily, and class imbalance, causing most GNNs to underperform in fraud detection tasks. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a Graph-Based Fraud Detection Model with Dual-Path Graph Filtering (DPF-GFD). DPF-GFD first applies a beta wavelet-based operator to the original graph to capture key structural patterns. It then constructs a similarity graph from distance-based node representations and applies an improved low-pass filter. The embeddings from the original and similarity graphs are fused through supervised representation learning to obtain node features, which are finally used by an ensemble tree model to assess the fraud risk of unlabeled nodes. Unlike existing single-graph smoothing approaches, DPF-GFD introduces a frequency-complementary dual-path filtering paradigm tailored for fraud detection, explicitly decoupling structural anomaly modeling and feature similarity modeling. This design enables more discriminative and stable node representations in highly heterophilous and imbalanced fraud graphs. Comprehensive experiments on four real-world financial fraud detection datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed method.

### [23] [Optimistic Policy Learning under Pessimistic Adversaries with Regret and Violation Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14243)
*Sourav Ganguly,Kartik Pandit,Arnob Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 首个研究显式对抗动力学下安全约束强化学习的工作，提出RHC-UCRL算法处理外部不可控因素对状态转移的影响


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实决策系统中状态转移不仅取决于智能体动作，还受外部不可控因素（竞争智能体、环境扰动、战略对手）影响。忽略这些因素可能导致孤立环境下最优但在部署中灾难性失败的策略，特别是在需要满足安全约束的场景中。标准约束MDP假设智能体是状态演化的唯一驱动因素，这在安全关键场景中不成立。

Method: 将外部因素建模为对抗策略π̄，共同决定状态转移。提出Robust Hallucinated Constrained Upper-Confidence RL (RHC-UCRL)算法，这是一种基于模型的方法，同时保持对智能体和对抗策略的乐观估计，明确分离认知不确定性和偶然不确定性。

Result: RHC-UCRL算法实现了次线性遗憾和约束违反保证。这是首个研究显式对抗动力学下安全约束强化学习的工作。

Conclusion: 通过显式建模外部因素为对抗策略，RHC-UCRL算法能够在存在不可控外部因素的环境中实现既优化又安全的决策，为安全关键场景中的强化学习提供了新的理论框架和算法保证。

Abstract: Real-world decision-making systems operate in environments where state transitions depend not only on the agent's actions, but also on \textbf{exogenous factors outside its control}--competing agents, environmental disturbances, or strategic adversaries--formally, $s_{h+1} = f(s_h, a_h, \bar{a}_h)+ω_h$ where $\bar{a}_h$ is the adversary/external action, $a_h$ is the agent's action, and $ω_h$ is an additive noise. Ignoring such factors can yield policies that are optimal in isolation but \textbf{fail catastrophically in deployment}, particularly when safety constraints must be satisfied.
  Standard Constrained MDP formulations assume the agent is the sole driver of state evolution, an assumption that breaks down in safety-critical settings. Existing robust RL approaches address this via distributional robustness over transition kernels, but do not explicitly model the \textbf{strategic interaction} between agent and exogenous factor, and rely on strong assumptions about divergence from a known nominal model.
  We model the exogenous factor as an \textbf{adversarial policy} $\barπ$ that co-determines state transitions, and ask how an agent can remain both optimal and safe against such an adversary. \emph{To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to study safety-constrained RL under explicit adversarial dynamics}. We propose \textbf{Robust Hallucinated Constrained Upper-Confidence RL} (\texttt{RHC-UCRL}), a model-based algorithm that maintains optimism over both agent and adversary policies, explicitly separating epistemic from aleatoric uncertainty. \texttt{RHC-UCRL} achieves sub-linear regret and constraint violation guarantees.

### [24] [Awakening Dormant Experts:Counterfactual Routing to Mitigate MoE Hallucinations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14246)

Method: 提出Counterfactual Routing (CoR)训练免费推理框架，结合层间扰动分析和反事实专家影响(CEI)度量，动态将计算资源从语法主导层转移到知识密集型层，通过虚拟消融检索因果决定性专家，同时保持总激活数不变

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models have achieved remarkable scalability, yet they remain vulnerable to hallucinations, particularly when processing long-tail knowledge. We identify that this fragility stems from static Top-$k$ routing: routers tend to favor high-frequency patterns over rare factual associations. Consequently, ``specialist experts'' possessing critical long-tail knowledge are often assigned low gating scores and remain ``dormant'' -- under-prioritized for specific tokens despite their proven causal importance on other inputs. To address this, we propose Counterfactual Routing (CoR), a training-free inference framework designed to awaken these dormant experts. CoR integrates layer-wise perturbation analysis with the Counterfactual Expert Impact (CEI) metric to dynamically shift computational resources from syntax-dominant to knowledge-intensive layers while maintaining a constant total activation count, effectively retrieving causally decisive experts via virtual ablation. Extensive experiments on TruthfulQA, FACTOR, and TriviaQA demonstrate that CoR improves factual accuracy by 3.1\% on average without increasing the inference budget, establishing a superior Pareto frontier compared to static scaling strategies.

### [25] [Metric-Aware Principal Component Analysis (MAPCA):A Unified Framework for Scale-Invariant Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14249)
*Michael Leznik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MAPCA是一个基于广义特征问题的尺度不变表示学习统一框架，通过度量矩阵M控制表示几何，连接了PCA、IPCA和多种自监督学习方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表示学习方法缺乏统一的几何框架来理解不同方法之间的关系，特别是尺度不变性、谱偏置控制和各种自监督学习目标之间的内在联系。

Method: 提出Metric-Aware PCA框架，基于广义特征问题max Tr(W^T Σ W) subject to W^T M W = I，其中M是对称正定度量矩阵。引入β族度量M(β)=Σ^β，β∈[0,1]提供连续谱偏置控制，对角线度量M=D=diag(Σ)恢复IPCA。

Result: 建立了统一框架连接多种方法：标准PCA(β=0)、输出白化(β=1)、IPCA(M=D)、Barlow Twins和ZCA白化(β=1)、VICReg方差项(对角线度量)。发现W-MSE对应M=Σ^{-1}(β=-1)，与Barlow Twins处于相反谱方向。

Conclusion: MAPCA提供了一个统一的几何语言，揭示了不同表示学习方法之间的深层联系，特别是输入白化和输出白化的区别在损失函数层面不可见，只有在MAPCA框架中才变得精确。

Abstract: We introduce Metric-Aware Principal Component Analysis (MAPCA), a unified framework for scale-invariant representation learning based on the generalised eigenproblem max Tr(W^T Sigma W) subject to W^T M W = I, where M is a symmetric positive definite metric matrix. The choice of M determines the representation geometry. The canonical beta-family M(beta) = Sigma^beta, beta in [0,1], provides continuous spectral bias control between standard PCA (beta=0) and output whitening (beta=1), with condition number kappa(beta) = (lambda_1/lambda_p)^(1-beta) decreasing monotonically to isotropy. The diagonal metric M = D = diag(Sigma) recovers Invariant PCA (IPCA), a method rooted in Frisch (1928) diagonal regression, as a distinct member of the broader framework. We prove that scale invariance holds if and only if the metric transforms as M_tilde = CMC under rescaling C, a condition satisfied exactly by IPCA but not by the general beta-family at intermediate values.
  Beyond its classical interpretation, MAPCA provides a geometric language that unifies several self-supervised learning objectives. Barlow Twins and ZCA whitening correspond to beta=1 (output whitening); VICReg's variance term corresponds to the diagonal metric. A key finding is that W-MSE, despite being described as a whitening-based method, corresponds to M = Sigma^{-1} (beta = -1), outside the spectral compression range entirely and in the opposite spectral direction to Barlow Twins. This distinction between input and output whitening is invisible at the level of loss functions and becomes precise only within the MAPCA framework.

</details>

Abstract: Applying kernel methods to matchings is challenging due to their discrete, non-Euclidean nature. In this paper, we develop a principled framework for constructing geometric kernels that respect the natural geometry of the space of matchings. To this end, we first provide a complete characterization of stationary kernels, i.e. kernels that respect the inherent symmetries of this space. Because the class of stationary kernels is too broad, we specifically focus on the heat and Matérn kernel families, adding an appropriate inductive bias of smoothness to stationarity. While these families successfully extend widely popular Euclidean kernels to matchings, evaluating them naively incurs a prohibitive super-exponential computational cost. To overcome this difficulty, we introduce and analyze a novel, sub-exponential algorithm leveraging zonal polynomials for efficient kernel evaluation. Finally, motivated by the known bijective correspondence between matchings and phylogenetic trees-a crucial data modality in biology-we explore whether our framework can be seamlessly transferred to the space of trees, establishing novel negative results and identifying a significant open problem.

### [27] [Calibrate-Then-Delegate: Safety Monitoring with Risk and Budget Guarantees via Model Cascades](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14251)
*Edoardo Pona,Milad Kazemi,Mehran Hosseini,Yali Du,David Watson,Osvaldo Simeone,Nicola Paoletti*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CTD是一种新型的LLM安全监控级联方法，通过直接预测升级价值而非不确定性来优化成本-准确率平衡，提供概率性计算成本保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于不确定性的级联方法存在缺陷：不确定性不能准确反映专家模型是否真正能纠正错误，导致资源分配效率低下。需要一种能直接预测升级价值的方法来优化成本-准确率平衡。

Method: 提出Calibrate-Then-Delegate (CTD)框架：1) 设计委托价值(DV)探针，基于安全探针的内部表示直接预测升级到专家模型的收益；2) 使用多重假设测试在校准数据上设置DV阈值，强制执行预算约束；3) 支持实例级(流式)决策，无需组标签。

Result: 在四个安全数据集上的评估表明：CTD在所有预算水平上都优于基于不确定性的委托方法；避免了有害的过度委托；能够根据输入难度自适应分配预算；提供有限样本保证。

Conclusion: CTD通过直接预测升级价值而非依赖不确定性，显著改善了LLM安全监控级联的成本-准确率权衡，为实际部署提供了具有概率保证的高效解决方案。

Abstract: Monitoring LLM safety at scale requires balancing cost and accuracy: a cheap latent-space probe can screen every input, but hard cases should be escalated to a more expensive expert. Existing cascades delegate based on probe uncertainty, but uncertainty is a poor proxy for delegation benefit, as it ignores whether the expert would actually correct the error. To address this problem, we introduce Calibrate-Then-Delegate (CTD), a model-cascade approach that provides probabilistic guarantees on the computation cost while enabling instance-level (streaming) decisions. CTD builds on a novel delegation value (DV) probe, a lightweight model operating on the same internal representations as the safety probe that directly predicts the benefit of escalation. To enforce budget constraints, CTD calibrates a threshold on the DV signal using held-out data via multiple hypothesis testing, yielding finite-sample guarantees on the delegation rate. Evaluated on four safety datasets, CTD consistently outperforms uncertainty-based delegation at every budget level, avoids harmful over-delegation, and adapts budget allocation to input difficulty without requiring group labels.

</details>


### [28] [Path-Sampled Integrated Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14338)
*Firuz Kamalov,Fadi Thabtah,R. Sivaraj,Neda Abdelhamid*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出路径采样积分梯度（PS-IG）框架，通过沿线性插值路径采样基线计算期望值来泛化特征归因，证明其与路径加权积分梯度的数学等价性，并展示其作为梯度噪声方差降低滤波器的功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有特征归因方法存在计算效率和方差问题。作者旨在开发一个框架，既能泛化特征归因方法，又能通过确定性计算提高收敛速度，同时降低梯度噪声引起的方差。

Method: 提出路径采样积分梯度（PS-IG）框架，通过沿线性插值路径采样基线计算期望值。证明当采样密度与加权函数匹配时，PS-IG与路径加权积分梯度数学等价。利用此等价性将随机期望转换为确定性黎曼和计算，并分析其作为方差降低滤波器的特性。

Result: PS-IG将误差收敛率从O(m^{-1/2})提升到O(m^{-1})（对平滑模型）。在均匀采样下，严格将归因方差降低1/3。同时保持线性、实现不变性等关键公理性质。

Conclusion: PS-IG提供了一个统一框架，既泛化了特征归因方法，又通过确定性计算提高了效率，同时作为有效的方差降低滤波器对抗梯度噪声，为可解释AI提供了理论保证和实用优势。

Abstract: We introduce path-sampled integrated gradients (PS-IG), a framework that generalizes feature attribution by computing the expected value over baselines sampled along the linear interpolation path. We prove that PS-IG is mathematically equivalent to path-weighted integrated gradients, provided the weighting function matches the cumulative distribution function of the sampling density. This equivalence allows the stochastic expectation to be evaluated via a deterministic Riemann sum, improving the error convergence rate from $O(m^{-1/2})$ to $O(m^{-1})$ for smooth models. Furthermore, we demonstrate analytically that PS-IG functions as a variance-reducing filter against gradient noise - strictly lowering attribution variance by a factor of 1/3 under uniform sampling - while preserving key axiomatic properties such as linearity and implementation invariance.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GUI grounding模型在标准基准测试中报告超过85%的准确率，但当指令需要空间推理而非直接元素命名时，性能下降27-56个百分点。当前基准测试因每个截图只使用单一固定指令进行评估而无法发现这一问题。

Method: 引入GUI-Perturbed框架，通过独立变化视觉场景和指令来测量grounding鲁棒性。评估了同一架构谱系的三个7B模型，包括测试关系指令、70%浏览器缩放效果，以及使用增强数据进行rank-8 LoRA微调的效果。

Result: 关系指令导致所有模型系统性准确率崩溃；70%浏览器缩放产生统计显著性能下降；使用增强数据的rank-8 LoRA微调反而降低了性能而非改善。通过独立扰动轴，GUI-Perturbed能够隔离特定能力轴（空间推理、视觉鲁棒性、推理校准）的影响。

Conclusion: GUI-Perturbed框架提供了聚合基准测试无法提供的诊断信号，揭示了现有GUI grounding模型在空间推理和视觉鲁棒性方面的系统性弱点。作者发布了数据集、增强管道和微调模型。

Abstract: GUI grounding models report over 85% accuracy on standard benchmarks, yet drop 27-56 percentage points when instructions require spatial reasoning rather than direct element naming. Current benchmarks miss this because they evaluate each screenshot once with a single fixed instruction. We introduce GUI-Perturbed, a controlled perturbation framework that independently varies visual scenes and instructions to measure grounding robustness. Evaluating three 7B models from the same architecture lineage, we find that relational instructions cause systematic accuracy collapse across all models, a 70% browser zoom produces statistically significant degradation, and rank-8 LoRA fine-tuning with augmented data degrades performance rather than improving it. By perturbing along independent axes, GUI-Perturbed isolates which specific capability axes are affected-spatial reasoning, visual robustness, reasoning calibration-providing diagnostic signal that aggregate benchmarks cannot. We release the dataset, augmentation pipeline, and a fine-tuned model.

### [30] [Tight Sample Complexity Bounds for Best-Arm Identification Under Bounded Systematic Bias](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14345)
*Tianhao Qian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在存在系统评估偏差的情况下，为自主推理和具身规划中的节点扩展提供形式化安全保证的方法，通过将节点扩展过程建模为带偏差的局部最佳臂识别问题，并推导出安全节点消除的样本复杂度边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自主推理和具身规划中搜索深度的增加，候选动作空间呈指数级扩展，严重消耗计算资源。虽然启发式剪枝是常见的对策，但当替代模型（如LLMs）存在系统评估偏差时，这种剪枝操作缺乏形式化的安全保证。因此需要一种能够在存在系统偏差的情况下，为节点扩展提供安全保证的方法。

Method: 将节点扩展过程建模为动态边界上的局部最佳臂识别问题，假设存在有界的系统偏差L。通过反演Lambert W函数，建立了加法样本复杂度为O((Δ-4L)^{-2})，表明只有当经验奖励差距超过4L时，安全节点消除才是可行的。同时提供了信息论下界Ω((Δ-2L)^{-2})来确认偏差搜索的结构限制。

Result: 在合成树和复杂推理任务上的评估表明，遵守这种局部安全边界能够成功保留最优轨迹，同时最大化样本分配效率。该方法在存在系统偏差的情况下，为节点扩展提供了形式化的安全保证。

Conclusion: 该研究为存在系统评估偏差的搜索过程提供了理论框架和安全边界，证明了当经验奖励差距超过偏差的四倍时，可以安全地进行节点消除，从而在保证最优性的同时提高搜索效率。

Abstract: As search depth increases in autonomous reasoning and embodied planning, the candidate action space expands exponentially, heavily taxing computational budgets. While heuristic pruning is a common countermeasure, it operates without formal safety guarantees when surrogate models (like LLMs) exhibit systematic evaluation biases. This paper frames the node expansion process as a localized Best-Arm Identification (BAI) problem over dynamic frontiers, subject to a bounded systematic bias $L$. By inverting the Lambert W function, we establish an additive sample complexity of $\mathcal{O}((Δ-4L)^{-2})$, which indicates that safe node elimination is only feasible when the empirical reward gap exceeds $4L$. We complement this with an information-theoretic lower bound of $Ω((Δ-2L)^{-2})$ to confirm the structural limits of biased search. Subsequent evaluations on both synthetic trees and complex reasoning tasks demonstrate that adhering to this local safety boundary successfully preserves optimal trajectories while maximizing sample allocation efficiency.

### [31] [Reinforcement Learning via Value Gradient Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14265)
*Haoran Xu,Kaiwen Hu,Somayeh Sojoudi,Amy Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VGF提出了一种基于最优传输的可扩展行为正则化强化学习新范式，通过离散梯度流将参考分布映射到价值诱导的最优策略分布，无需显式策略参数化


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有行为正则化RL方法存在局限性：基于重参数化策略梯度的方法难以扩展到大型生成模型，而拒绝采样方法在尝试超越行为支持时可能过于保守。需要一种既可扩展又不过度保守的新方法来解决价值过度优化问题

Method: 将行为正则化RL建模为最优传输问题，将参考分布映射到价值诱导的最优策略分布。通过离散梯度流求解，其中价值梯度引导从参考分布初始化的粒子。通过控制传输预算实现隐式正则化，无需显式策略参数化

Result: 在离线RL基准（D4RL、OGBench）和LLM RL任务上显著优于现有方法，达到最先进水平。VGF能够通过调整传输预算实现自适应测试时缩放

Conclusion: VGF为行为正则化RL提供了一个可扩展、灵活且表达力强的新范式，通过最优传输框架有效解决了现有方法的局限性，在多个领域取得了优异性能

Abstract: We study behavior-regularized reinforcement learning (RL), where regularization toward a reference distribution (the dataset in offline RL or the base model in LLM RL finetuning) is essential to prevent value over-optimization caused by erroneous out-of-distribution extrapolation. Existing methods either rely on reparameterized policy gradient, which are difficult to scale to large generative models, or on reject sampling, which can be overly conservative when attempting to move beyond the behavior support. In this paper, we propose Value Gradient Flow (VGF), a scalable new paradigm for behavior-regularized RL. VGF casts behavior-regularized RL as an optimal transport problem that maps the reference distribution to the value-induced optimal policy distribution. We solve this transport problem via discrete gradient flow, where value gradients guide particles initialized from the reference distribution. Our analysis shows that VGF imposes regularization implicitly by controlling the transport budget. VGF eliminates explicit policy parameterization while remaining expressive and flexible, this enables adaptive test-time scaling by adjusting the transport budget. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VGF significantly outperforms prior methods, achieving state-of-the-art results on offline RL benchmarks (D4RL, OGBench) and LLM RL tasks. Code and runs can be found at https://ryanxhr.github.io/vgf.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有搜索代理训练方法存在局限：过程监督常面临不稳定的价值估计，而结果监督由于稀疏的轨迹级奖励难以进行信用分配。需要弥合这一差距，实现更稳定和细粒度的搜索代理训练。

Method: 提出贡献加权GRPO框架，使用LLM法官评估每轮搜索的检索效用和推理正确性，生成每轮贡献分数。这些分数用于重新调整基于结果的轨迹优势，将过程监督整合到组相对策略优化中。

Abstract: Search agents extend Large Language Models (LLMs) beyond static parametric knowledge by enabling access to up-to-date and long-tail information unavailable during pretraining. While reinforcement learning has been widely adopted for training such agents, existing approaches face key limitations: process supervision often suffers from unstable value estimation, whereas outcome supervision struggles with credit assignment due to sparse, trajectory-level rewards. To bridge this gap, we propose Contribution-Weighted GRPO (CW-GRPO), a framework that integrates process supervision into group relative policy optimization. Instead of directly optimizing process rewards, CW-GRPO employs an LLM judge to assess the retrieval utility and reasoning correctness at each search round, producing per-round contribution scores. These scores are used to rescale outcome-based advantages along the trajectory, enabling fine-grained credit assignment without sacrificing optimization stability. Experiments on multiple knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that CW-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO by 5.0\% on Qwen3-8B and 6.3\% on Qwen3-1.7B, leading to more effective search behaviors. Additional analysis reveals that successful trajectories exhibit concentrated contributions across rounds, providing empirical insight into search agent tasks.

### [33] [CLion: Efficient Cautious Lion Optimizer with Enhanced Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14587)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lion优化器在深度学习训练中表现出色，但其泛化分析尚未被研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，分析Lion的泛化性能，并设计具有更好泛化能力的改进版本。

Method: 基于数学归纳法的算法稳定性分析Lion的泛化误差；设计CLion优化器，通过谨慎使用符号函数来增强泛化；理论分析CLion的收敛性和泛化性能。

Result: 证明了Lion的泛化误差为O(1/(Nτ^T))，其中τ为梯度估计器中非零元素的最小绝对值；发现SignSGD具有与Lion相同的泛化误差；CLion具有更低的泛化误差O(1/N)和O(√d/T^{1/4})的收敛速度。

Conclusion: 本文首次分析了Lion优化器的泛化性能，提出的CLion优化器在保持快速收敛的同时显著改善了泛化能力，为基于符号的优化算法提供了理论保证。

Abstract: Lion optimizer is a popular learning-based optimization algorithm in machine learning, which shows impressive performance in training many deep learning models. Although convergence property of the Lion optimizer has been studied, its generalization analysis is still missing. To fill this gap, we study generalization property of the Lion via algorithmic stability based on the mathematical induction. Specifically, we prove that the Lion has a generalization error of $O(\frac{1}{Nτ^T})$, where $N$ is training sample size, and $τ>0$ denotes the smallest absolute value of non-zero element in gradient estimator, and $T$ is the total iteration number. In addition, we obtain an interesting byproduct that the SignSGD algorithm has the same generalization error as the Lion. To enhance generalization of the Lion, we design a novel efficient Cautious Lion (i.e., CLion) optimizer by cautiously using sign function. Moreover, we prove that our CLion has a lower generalization error of $O(\frac{1}{N})$ than $O(\frac{1}{Nτ^T})$ of the Lion, since the parameter $τ$ generally is very small. Meanwhile, we study convergence property of our CLion optimizer, and prove that our CLion has a fast convergence rate of $O(\frac{\sqrt{d}}{T^{1/4}})$ under $\ell_1$-norm of gradient for nonconvex stochastic optimization, where $d$ denotes the model dimension.
  Extensive numerical experiments demonstrate effectiveness of our CLion optimizer.

### [34] [Generative Augmented Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14575)
*Cheng Lu,Mengxin Wang,Dennis J. Zhang,Heng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Generative Augmented Inference (GAI)框架，将AI生成输出作为特征而非标签代理，通过正交矩构造实现灵活非参数关系下的估计和推断

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Generative Augmented Inference (GAI)框架，将AI生成输出作为估计人工标签模型的信息特征而非直接代理。采用正交矩构造，允许LLM生成输出与人工标签之间灵活的非参数关系，实现一致估计和有效推断。

Result: 理论证明渐近正态性和"安全默认"特性：相对于仅使用人工数据的估计器，GAI在任意辅助信号下弱改进估计效率，当辅助信息具有预测性时获得严格增益。实证表明：在弱辅助信号的联合分析中减少约50%估计误差，降低75%以上人工标注需求；在零售定价中优于所有替代估计器；在健康保险选择中减少90%以上标注需求同时保持决策准确性；所有应用中改进置信区间覆盖而不增加宽度。

Conclusion: GAI为整合AI生成信息提供了原则性和可扩展的方法，通过将AI输出作为特征而非标签代理，利用正交矩构造实现灵活关系下的高效估计和可靠推断，显著降低人工标注成本同时提高估计精度。

Abstract: Data-driven operations management often relies on parameters estimated from costly human-generated labels. Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) and other AI systems offer inexpensive auxiliary data, but introduce a new challenge: AI outputs are not direct observations of the target outcomes, but could involve high-dimensional representations with complex and unknown relationships to human labels. Conventional methods leverage AI predictions as direct proxies for true labels, which can be inefficient or unreliable when this relationship is weak or misspecified. We propose Generative Augmented Inference (GAI), a general framework that incorporates AI-generated outputs as informative features for estimating models of human-labeled outcomes. GAI uses an orthogonal moment construction that enables consistent estimation and valid inference with flexible, nonparametric relationship between LLM-generated outputs and human labels. We establish asymptotic normality and show a "safe default" property: relative to human-data-only estimators, GAI weakly improves estimation efficiency under arbitrary auxiliary signals and yields strict gains whenever the auxiliary information is predictive. Empirically, GAI outperforms benchmarks across diverse settings. In conjoint analysis with weak auxiliary signals, GAI reduces estimation error by about 50% and lowers human labeling requirements by over 75%. In retail pricing, where all methods access the same auxiliary inputs, GAI consistently outperforms alternative estimators, highlighting the value of its construction rather than differences in information. In health insurance choice, it cuts labeling requirements by over 90% while maintaining decision accuracy. Across applications, GAI improves confidence interval coverage without inflating width. Overall, GAI provides a principled and scalable approach to integrating AI-generated information.

### [35] [Quantum-inspired tensor networks in machine learning models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14287)
*Guillermo Valverde,Igor García-Olaizola,Giannicola Scarpa,Alejandro Pozas-Kerstjens*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文综述了张量网络在机器学习中的应用，评估了其作为替代学习架构和神经网络组件分解的潜力，并分析了其在计算效率、可解释性和隐私方面的优势与挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张量网络最初在量子多体物理中发展，用于压缩表示多粒子量子态，通过捕捉最相关的依赖关系来缓解多体系统的指数复杂度。由于量子纠缠与统计相关性之间的形式相似性，张量网络最近被整合到机器学习中，既可作为替代学习架构，也可作为神经网络组件的分解方法。期望利用量子多体物理中发展的张量网络理论理解，开发出在计算效率、可解释性或隐私方面具有优势的新方法。

Method: 本文采用综述研究方法，系统回顾了张量网络在机器学习领域的应用。首先介绍了张量网络在量子多体物理中的起源和基本原理，然后分析了其与机器学习结合的理论基础——量子纠缠与统计相关性的形式相似性。接着分类讨论了张量网络在机器学习中的两种主要应用模式：作为替代学习架构和作为神经网络组件的分解方法。

Result: 通过对现有文献的系统回顾，本文提供了张量网络在机器学习中应用现状的全面评估。分析了张量网络方法在计算效率方面的潜在优势，包括参数压缩和计算复杂度降低；在可解释性方面的改进，源于张量网络的物理可解释结构；以及在隐私保护方面的潜力，基于张量网络的分布式表示特性。同时识别了当前面临的挑战，包括理论框架的完善、实际应用的扩展性以及与传统深度学习方法的效果对比。

Conclusion: 张量网络为机器学习提供了有前景的新范式，有望在计算效率、可解释性和隐私保护方面带来实质性改进。然而，要实现这些潜力，需要克服理论理解与实际应用之间的差距，开发更有效的训练算法，并在更广泛的机器学习任务中验证其性能。未来的研究应关注于建立更坚实的理论基础，开发实用的实现方法，并探索张量网络与现有机器学习技术的深度融合。

Abstract: Tensor networks were developed in the context of many-body physics as compressed representations of multiparticle quantum states. These representations mitigate the exponential complexity of many-body systems by capturing only the most relevant dependencies. Due to the formal similarity between quantum entanglement and statistical correlations, tensor networks have recently been integrated in machine learning, operating both as alternative learning architectures and as decompositions of components of neural networks. The expectation is that the theoretical understanding of tensor networks developed within quantum many-body physics leads to novel methods that offer advantages in terms of computational efficiency, explainability, or privacy. Here we review the use of tensor networks in the context of machine learning, providing a critical assessment of the state of the art, the potential advantages, and the challenges that must be overcome.

### [36] [Zeroth-Order Optimization at the Edge of Stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14669)
*Minhak Song,Liang Zhang,Bingcong Li,Niao He,Michael Muehlebach,Sewoong Oh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文分析了基于标准两点估计器的零阶方法的稳定性条件，揭示了其与一阶方法的本质差异：一阶方法稳定性仅由最大Hessian特征值决定，而零阶方法稳定性取决于整个Hessian谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零阶方法在梯度不可用或计算成本过高时被广泛应用，但在深度学习中的优化动力学研究不足。本文旨在揭示零阶方法的稳定性特性及其与一阶方法的根本差异。

Method: 提出了基于标准两点估计器的零阶方法的显式步长条件，精确刻画其均方线性稳定性。由于计算完整Hessian谱在实际神经网络训练中不可行，进一步推导了仅依赖于最大特征值和Hessian迹的可处理稳定性边界。

Result: 发现全批量零阶方法在稳定性边缘运行：ZO-GD、ZO-GDM和ZO-Adam在一系列深度学习训练问题中始终稳定在预测的稳定性边界附近。揭示了零阶方法特有的隐式正则化效应：大步长主要正则化Hessian迹，而一阶方法中则正则化最大特征值。

Conclusion: 零阶方法的稳定性特性与一阶方法存在根本差异，这种差异导致了不同的隐式正则化机制。研究结果为理解零阶优化在深度学习中的行为提供了理论基础，并揭示了其特有的正则化特性。

Abstract: Zeroth-order (ZO) methods are widely used when gradients are unavailable or prohibitively expensive, including black-box learning and memory-efficient fine-tuning of large models, yet their optimization dynamics in deep learning remain underexplored. In this work, we provide an explicit step size condition that exactly captures the (mean-square) linear stability of a family of ZO methods based on the standard two-point estimator. Our characterization reveals a sharp contrast with first-order (FO) methods: whereas FO stability is governed solely by the largest Hessian eigenvalue, mean-square stability of ZO methods depends on the entire Hessian spectrum. Since computing the full Hessian spectrum is infeasible in practical neural network training, we further derive tractable stability bounds that depend only on the largest eigenvalue and the Hessian trace. Empirically, we find that full-batch ZO methods operate at the edge of stability: ZO-GD, ZO-GDM, and ZO-Adam consistently stabilize near the predicted stability boundary across a range of deep learning training problems. Our results highlight an implicit regularization effect specific to ZO methods, where large step sizes primarily regularize the Hessian trace, whereas in FO methods they regularize the top eigenvalue.

*Mathias Dus*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强化学习方法缺乏几何视角，该研究旨在为RL建立一个几何框架，将策略视为映射到Wasserstein概率空间的函数，从而利用微分几何工具进行策略优化分析。

Method: 1) 定义由平稳分布诱导的黎曼结构；2) 定义策略的切空间并刻画测地线；3) 构建一般RL优化问题并使用Otto微积分构造梯度流；4) 计算能量函数的梯度和Hessian矩阵；5) 对低维问题直接计算梯度，对高维问题使用神经网络参数化策略并基于遍历近似进行优化。

Result: 1) 证明了在一般背景下平稳分布诱导的黎曼结构的存在性；2) 完整刻画了策略切空间和测地线；3) 提供了能量函数梯度和Hessian的形式化二阶分析；4) 通过数值示例验证了理论框架的有效性，包括低维问题的直接梯度计算和高维问题的神经网络优化。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了一个将强化学习策略几何化的理论框架，为策略优化提供了新的微分几何视角和数学工具，能够处理从低维到高维的RL问题，并为二阶优化方法奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present a geometric framework for Reinforcement Learning (RL) that views policies as maps into the Wasserstein space of action probabilities. First, we define a Riemannian structure induced by stationary distributions, proving its existence in a general context. We then define the tangent space of policies and characterize the geodesics, specifically addressing the measurability of vector fields mapped from the state space to the tangent space of probability measures over the action space. Next, we formulate a general RL optimization problem and construct a gradient flow using Otto's calculus. We compute the gradient and the Hessian of the energy, providing a formal second-order analysis. Finally, we illustrate the method with numerical examples for low-dimensional problems, computing the gradient directly from our theoretical formalism. For high-dimensional problems, we parameterize the policy using a neural network and optimize it based on an ergodic approximation of the cost.

### [38] [Thermodynamic Diffusion Inference with Minimal Digital Conditioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14332)
*Aditi De*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出基于热力学扩散推理的物理计算系统，通过层次双线性耦合解决U-Net跳跃连接问题，使用极小数字接口克服条件限制，实现比GPU推理节能约1000万倍的生产级热力学扩散推理


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型推理与过阻尼朗之万动力学在形式上是等价的，因此编码得分函数的物理基底仅通过热力学就能平衡到正确输出，无需数字算术运算，理论上比GPU节能10000倍。但存在两个主要障碍：非局部跳跃连接（局部耦合的模拟基底无法表示）和输入条件（耦合常数信号强度不足2600倍）

Method: 1. 层次双线性耦合：将U-Net跳跃连接编码为从编码器和解码器Gram矩阵奇异结构导出的秩-k模块间相互作用，仅需O(Dk)物理连接而非O(D²)。2. 极小数字接口：包含4维瓶颈编码器和16单元传输网络，总计2560个参数，克服条件限制障碍

Result: 在从训练好的去噪U-Net提取的激活上评估，完整系统达到解码器余弦相似度0.9906（理论上限为1.0000），同时保持约10⁷倍的理论净节能效果（相比GPU推理）

Abstract: Diffusion-model inference and overdamped Langevin dynamics are formally identical. A physical substrate that encodes the score function therefore equilibrates to the correct output by thermodynamics alone, requiring no digital arithmetic during inference and potentially achieving a $10{,}000\times$ reduction in energy relative to a GPU. Two fundamental barriers have until now prevented this equivalence from being realized at production scale: non-local skip connections, which locally coupled analog substrates cannot represent, and input conditioning, in which the coupling constants carry roughly $2{,}600\times$ too little signal to anchor the system to a specific input.
  We resolve both obstacles. \emph{Hierarchical bilinear coupling} encodes U-Net skip connections as rank-$k$ inter-module interactions derived directly from the singular structure of the encoder and decoder Gram matrices, requiring only $O(Dk)$ physical connections instead of $O(D^2)$. A \emph{minimal digital interface} -- a 4-dimensional bottleneck encoder together with a 16-unit transfer network, totalling \textbf{2,560 parameters} -- overcomes the conditioning barrier. When evaluated on activations drawn from a trained denoising U-Net, the complete system attains a decoder cosine similarity of \textbf{0.9906} against an oracle upper bound of 1.0000, while preserving theoretical net energy savings of approximately $10^7\times$ over GPU inference. These results constitute the first demonstration of trained-weight, production-scale thermodynamic diffusion inference.

Result: 理论分析表明门控注意力在几何表达能力上存在优势：无门控注意力仅限于平坦统计流形，而门控注意力能够产生非平坦几何，包括正曲率流形。实证结果显示，门控模型在需要非线性决策边界的任务上表现出更高的表示曲率和更好的性能，但在线性决策边界任务上没有一致优势。此外，研究发现存在一种结构化机制，使得曲率在组合过程中累积，产生系统性的深度放大效应。

Conclusion: 乘法门控通过改变注意力表示空间的几何结构来增强模型的表达能力，特别是通过引入非平坦（正曲率）统计流形。这种几何表达能力差距解释了门控注意力在复杂任务上的性能优势，并为理解深度神经网络中表示几何的演化提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Multiplicative gating is widely used in neural architectures and has recently been applied to attention layers to improve performance and training stability in large language models. Despite the success of gated attention, the mathematical implications of gated attention mechanisms remain poorly understood. We study attention through the geometry of its representations by modeling outputs as mean parameters of Gaussian distributions and analyzing the induced Fisher--Rao geometry. We show that ungated attention operator is restricted to intrinsically flat statistical manifolds due to its affine structure, while multiplicative gating enables non-flat geometries, including positively curved manifolds that are unattainable in the ungated setting. These results establish a geometric expressivity gap between ungated and gated attention. Empirically, we show that gated models exhibit higher representation curvature and improved performance on tasks requiring nonlinear decision boundaries whereas they provide no consistent advantage on tasks with linear decision boundaries. Furthermore, we identify a structured regime in which curvature accumulates under composition, yielding a systematic depth amplification effect.

### [41] [Multi-User mmWave Beam and Rate Adaptation via Combinatorial Satisficing Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14908)

BSs learn about transmission success based on ACK/NACK feedback. To encode service goals, we introduce a satisficing throughput threshold $τ_r$ and cast joint beam and rate adaptation as a combinatorial semi-bandit over beam-rate tuples. Within this framework, we propose SAT-CTS, a lightweight, threshold-aware policy that blends conservative confidence estimates with posterior sampling, steering learning toward meeting $τ_r$ rather than merely maximizing. Our main theoretical contribution provides the first finite-time regret bounds for combinatorial semi-bandits with satisficing objective: when $τ_r$ is realizable, we upper bound the cumulative satisficing regret to the target with a time-independent constant, and when $τ_r$ is non-realizable, we show that SAT-CTS incurs only a finite expected transient outside committed CTS rounds, after which its regret is governed by the sum of the regret contributions of restarted CTS rounds, yielding an $O((\log T)^2)$ standard regret bound. On the practical side, we evaluate the performance via cumulative satisficing regret to $τ_r$ alongside standard regret and fairness. Experiments with time-varying sparse multipath channels show that SAT-CTS consistently reduces satisficing regret and maintains competitive standard regret, while achieving favorable average throughput and fairness across users, indicating that feedback-efficient learning can equitably allocate beams and rates to meet QoS targets without channel state knowledge.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类偏好本质上是多元的，对齐模型需要平衡多个下游目标（如美学质量和图文一致性）。现有多目标方法要么依赖昂贵的多目标RL微调，要么在去噪时融合单独对齐的模型，通常需要奖励值（或其梯度）访问权限和/或引入近似误差。

Method: 重新审视扩散模型的RL微调问题，引入步级RL公式解决最优策略识别难题。在此基础上提出MSDDA（多目标步级去噪时扩散对齐）框架，无需重新训练即可对齐扩散模型与多个目标，获得闭式形式的最优反向去噪分布，其均值和方差直接由单目标基础模型表达。

Result: 证明该去噪时目标与步级RL微调完全等价，不引入任何近似误差。数值结果表明该方法优于现有的去噪时方法。

Conclusion: MSDDA提供了一种无需重新训练的多目标对齐框架，通过步级RL公式获得闭式最优解，在保持理论精确性的同时提升了多目标对齐的性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful tool for aligning diffusion models with human preferences, typically by optimizing a single reward function under a KL regularization constraint. In practice, however, human preferences are inherently pluralistic, and aligned models must balance multiple downstream objectives, such as aesthetic quality and text-image consistency. Existing multi-objective approaches either rely on costly multi-objective RL fine-tuning or on fusing separately aligned models at denoising time, but they generally require access to reward values (or their gradients) and/or introduce approximation error in the resulting denoising objectives. In this paper, we revisit the problem of RL fine-tuning for diffusion models and address the intractability of identifying the optimal policy by introducing a step-level RL formulation. Building on this, we further propose Multi-objective Step-level Denoising-time Diffusion Alignment (MSDDA), a retraining-free framework for aligning diffusion models with multiple objectives, obtaining the optimal reverse denoising distribution in closed form, with mean and variance expressed directly in terms of single-objective base models. We prove that this denoising-time objective is exactly equivalent to the step-level RL fine-tuning, introducing no approximation error. Moreover, we provide numerical results, which indicate our method outperforms existing denoising-time approaches.

However, these simulations are often high-fidelity in nature, and can be computationally very expensive. Hence, generating data from these expensive simulations becomes a bottleneck in an end-to-end engineering design process. Spatio-temporal surrogate modeling of these dynamical systems has been a popular data-driven solution to tackle this computational bottleneck. This is because accurate machine learning models emulating the dynamical systems can be orders of magnitude faster than the actual simulations. However, one key limitation of purely data-driven approaches is their lack of generalizability to inputs outside the training distribution. In this paper, we propose a physics-informed spatio-temporal surrogate modeling (PISTM) framework constrained by the physics of the underlying dynamical system. We evaluate our framework on a prototypical fluid flow problem of interest: two-dimensional incompressible flow around a cylinder.

### [46] [Auxiliary Finite-Difference Residual-Gradient Regularization for PINNs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14472)
*Stavros Kassinos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种混合PINN设计，其中PDE残差保持自动微分计算，而有限差分仅用于弱辅助项来惩罚残差场的梯度，以此正则化残差场而不替代PDE残差本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统PINN通常使用单一标量损失函数，即使关注的具体物理量更为特定。本研究旨在探索一种混合设计，在保持自动微分计算PDE残差的同时，引入有限差分作为弱辅助项来正则化残差场，以提高特定物理量的预测精度。

Method: 采用两阶段实验设计：第一阶段在受控泊松基准问题中比较基线PINN、FD残差梯度正则器和匹配的AD残差梯度基线；第二阶段将相同逻辑应用于三维环形热传导基准问题（PINN3D），其中基线误差集中在波浪形外壁附近，辅助网格实现为壁面相邻的贴体壳层。

Result: 在阶段1中，FD正则器重现了残差梯度控制的主要效果，同时揭示了场精度与残差清洁度之间的权衡。在阶段2中，壳层正则器改善了应用相关量，即外壁通量和边界条件行为。在种子0-5和100k轮次下，最可靠的配置是在Kourkoutas-beta优化器下固定壳层权重为5e-4：相对于无壳层项的匹配运行，它将平均外壁BC RMSE从1.22e-2降低到9.29e-4，平均壁通量RMSE从9.21e-3降低到9.63e-4。

Conclusion: 结果支持混合PINN的针对性观点：当辅助FD正则器与感兴趣的物理量（此处为外壁通量）对齐时，其价值最大。该方法在保持自动微分计算PDE残差的同时，通过有限差分正则化残差场，有效提高了特定物理量的预测精度。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) are often selected by a single scalar loss even when the quantity of interest is more specific. We study a hybrid design in which the governing PDE residual remains automatic-differentiation (AD) based, while finite differences (FD) appear only in a weak auxiliary term that penalizes gradients of the sampled residual field. The FD term regularizes the residual field without replacing the PDE residual itself.
  We examine this idea in two stages. Stage 1 is a controlled Poisson benchmark comparing a baseline PINN, the FD residual-gradient regularizer, and a matched AD residual-gradient baseline. Stage 2 transfers the same logic to a three-dimensional annular heat-conduction benchmark (PINN3D), where baseline errors concentrate near a wavy outer wall and the auxiliary grid is implemented as a body-fitted shell adjacent to the wall.
  In Stage 1, the FD regularizer reproduces the main effect of residual-gradient control while exposing a trade-off between field accuracy and residual cleanliness. In Stage 2, the shell regularizer improves the application-facing quantities, namely outer-wall flux and boundary-condition behavior. Across seeds 0-5 and 100k epochs, the most reliable tested configuration is a fixed shell weight of 5e-4 under the Kourkoutas-beta optimizer regime: relative to a matched run without the shell term, it reduces the mean outer-wall BC RMSE from 1.22e-2 to 9.29e-4 and the mean wall-flux RMSE from 9.21e-3 to 9.63e-4. Adam with beta2=0.999 becomes usable when the initial learning rate is reduced to 1e-3, although its shell benefit is less robust than under Kourkoutas-beta. Overall, the results support a targeted view of hybrid PINNs: an auxiliary-only FD regularizer is most valuable when it is aligned with the physical quantity of interest, here the outer-wall flux.

*Evan Gibson Smith,Jacob Whitehill,Fatemeh Ganji*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SNN量化评估主要关注精度，忽视了量化是否保持全精度网络的脉冲行为，而脉冲行为直接影响部署中的稀疏性、状态存储和事件处理负载。

Result: 均匀量化即使精度保持不变也会导致分布漂移，而LQ-Net风格的学习量化能保持接近全精度基线的脉冲行为。

Abstract: Quantization is a natural complement to the sparse, event-driven computation of Spiking Neural Networks, reducing memory bandwidth and arithmetic cost for deployment on resource-constrained hardware. However, existing SNN quantization evaluation focuses almost exclusively on accuracy, overlooking whether a quantized network preserves the firing behavior of its full-precision counterpart. We demonstrate that quantization method, clipping range, and bit-width can produce substantially different firing distributions at equivalent accuracy, differences invisible to standard metrics but relevant to deployment, where firing activity governs effective sparsity, state storage, and event-processing load. To capture this gap, we propose Earth Mover's Distance as a diagnostic metric for firing distribution divergence, and apply it systematically across weight and membrane quantization on SEW-ResNet architectures trained on CIFAR-10 and CIFAR-100. We find that uniform quantization induces distributional drift even when accuracy is preserved, while LQ-Net style learned quantization maintains firing behavior close to the full-precision baseline. Our results suggest that behavior preservation should be treated as an evaluation criterion alongside accuracy, and that EMD provides a principled tool for assessing it.

### [49] [On the Expressive Power and Limitations of Multi-Layer SSMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14501)
*Nikola Zubić,Qian Li,Yuyi Wang,Davide Scaramuzza*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 多层级状态空间模型（SSMs）在组合任务中存在固有局限性，与流式模型存在表达力差距；离线思维链（CoT）无法根本提升表达力，而在线CoT能显著增强SSMs能力，使其达到流式算法同等水平；宽度与精度在基础模型中不可互换，但引入在线CoT后实现等价转换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多层状态空间模型的表达能力和局限性，探索深度、有限精度和思维链如何共同塑造SSMs的能力边界，为理解SSMs的理论基础提供统一视角。

Method: 通过理论分析研究多层SSMs的表达能力：1）证明多层SSMs在组合任务中的固有局限性；2）分析离线与在线思维链对SSMs表达力的不同影响；3）探究宽度与精度资源在基础模型和CoT增强模型中的可互换性。

Result: 1）多层SSMs在组合任务中存在表达力差距，无法达到流式模型水平；2）离线CoT无法根本提升SSMs表达力，而在线CoT能显著增强其能力，使多层SSMs达到流式算法同等表达能力；3）宽度与精度在基础模型中不可互换，但引入在线CoT后实现等价转换。

Abstract: We study the expressive power and limitations of multi-layer state-space models (SSMs). First, we show that multi-layer SSMs face fundamental limitations in compositional tasks, revealing an inherent gap between SSMs and streaming models. Then, we examine the role of chain-of-thought (CoT), showing that offline CoT does not fundamentally increase the expressiveness, while online CoT can substantially increase its power. Indeed, with online CoT, multi-layer SSMs become equivalent in power to streaming algorithms. Finally, we investigate the tradeoff between width and precision, showing that these resources are not interchangeable in the base model, but admit a clean equivalence once online CoT is allowed. Overall, our results offer a unified perspective on how depth, finite precision, and CoT shape the power and limits of SSMs.

### [50] [CI-CBM: Class-Incremental Concept Bottleneck Model for Interpretable Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14519)

Abstract: Catastrophic forgetting remains a fundamental challenge in continual learning, in which models often forget previous knowledge when fine-tuned on a new task. This issue is especially pronounced in class incremental learning (CIL), which is the most challenging setting in continual learning. Existing methods to address catastrophic forgetting often sacrifice either model interpretability or accuracy. To address this challenge, we introduce ClassIncremental Concept Bottleneck Model (CI-CBM), which leverage effective techniques, including concept regularization and pseudo-concept generation to maintain interpretable decision processes throughout incremental learning phases. Through extensive evaluation on seven datasets, CI-CBM achieves comparable performance to black-box models and outperforms previous interpretable approaches in CIL, with an average 36% accuracy gain. CICBM provides interpretable decisions on individual inputs and understandable global decision rules, as shown in our experiments, thereby demonstrating that human understandable concepts can be maintained during incremental learning without compromising model performance. Our approach is effective in both pretrained and non-pretrained scenarios; in the latter, the backbone is trained from scratch during the first learning phase. Code is publicly available at github.com/importAmir/CI-CBM.

### [51] [CSRA: Controlled Spectral Residual Augmentation for Robust Sepsis Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14532)
*Honglin Guo,Rihao Chang,He Jiao,Weizhi Nie,Zhongheng Zhang,Yuehao Shen*

TL;DR: CSRA是一个用于ICU短窗口多系统时间序列预测的受控谱残差增强框架，通过系统级表示和谱域扰动生成临床合理的轨迹变化，提升脓毒症风险预测性能。
