<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型在医学影像解读中通常将临床医生置于被动观察者位置，缺乏可解释的推理痕迹供医生检查、验证或改进。需要一种能够提供透明决策过程的AI系统。

Method: 引入RadAgent，一种工具使用的AI代理，通过逐步、可解释的过程生成CT报告。系统生成完全可检查的中间决策和工具交互痕迹，使临床医生能够检查报告结果的推导过程。

Result: RadAgent在三个维度上优于其3D VLM对应物CT-Chat：临床准确性（宏F1提高6.0点，相对36.4%；微F1提高5.4点，相对19.6%）；对抗条件下的鲁棒性提高24.7点（相对41.9%）；忠实度达到37.0%，这是其3D VLM对应物完全不具备的新能力。

Conclusion: 通过将胸部CT解读构建为显式、工具增强和迭代的推理痕迹，RadAgent使我们更接近透明可靠的放射学AI，为临床医生提供了可检查、验证和精炼的决策过程。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLM) have markedly advanced AI-driven interpretation and reporting of complex medical imaging, such as computed tomography (CT). Yet, existing methods largely relegate clinicians to passive observers of final outputs, offering no interpretable reasoning trace for them to inspect, validate, or refine. To address this, we introduce RadAgent, a tool-using AI agent that generates CT reports through a stepwise and interpretable process. Each resulting report is accompanied by a fully inspectable trace of intermediate decisions and tool interactions, allowing clinicians to examine how the reported findings are derived. In our experiments, we observe that RadAgent improves Chest CT report generation over its 3D VLM counterpart, CT-Chat, across three dimensions. Clinical accuracy improves by 6.0 points (36.4% relative) in macro-F1 and 5.4 points (19.6% relative) in micro-F1. Robustness under adversarial conditions improves by 24.7 points (41.9% relative). Furthermore, RadAgent achieves 37.0% in faithfulness, a new capability entirely absent in its 3D VLM counterpart. By structuring the interpretation of chest CT as an explicit, tool-augmented and iterative reasoning trace, RadAgent brings us closer toward transparent and reliable AI for radiology.

### [192] [Blue Data Intelligence Layer: Streaming Data and Agents for Multi-source Multi-modal Data-Centric Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15233)
*Moin Aminnaseri,Farima Fatahi Bayat,Nikita Bhutani,Jean-Flavien Bussotti,Kevin Chan,Rafael Li Chen,Yanlin Feng,Jackson Hassell,Estevam Hruschka,Eser Kandogan,Hannah Kim,James Levine,Seiji Maekawa,Jalal Mahmud,Kushan Mitra,Naoki Otani,Pouya Pezeshkpour,Nima Shahbazi,Chen Shen,Dan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Blue的DIL是一个复合AI系统，旨在超越传统的单数据库NL2SQL，通过统一结构化企业数据、LLM世界知识和交互获取的个人上下文，支持多源、多模态的数据中心应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的信息需求很少能映射到单个SQL查询，因为用户查询是迭代表达的、问题常涉及多个数据源、且查询依赖常识或外部知识。需要整合异构源、多模态和上下文数据来满足实际数据需求。

Method: DIL作为数据智能层，包含数据注册表存储多源多模态元数据，将LLM、Web和用户视为"数据库"源。使用数据规划器将用户查询转换为可执行查询计划，这些计划是统一关系运算符和多模态运算符的声明性抽象，支持复杂请求分解、多源检索和推理集成。

Result: 通过两个交互场景展示了DIL如何动态触发多源检索、跨模态推理和结果合成，说明复合AI系统如何超越单数据库NL2SQL。

Conclusion: DIL通过统一结构化企业数据、LLM世界知识和个人上下文，桥接用户意图与可用信息之间的语义鸿沟，为面向企业的复合AI系统提供了数据智能层，支持多源多模态的数据中心应用。

Abstract: NL2SQL systems aim to address the growing need for natural language interaction with data. However, real-world information rarely maps to a single SQL query because (1) users express queries iteratively (2) questions often span multiple data sources beyond the closed-world assumption of a single database, and (3) queries frequently rely on commonsense or external knowledge. Consequently, satisfying realistic data needs require integrating heterogeneous sources, modalities, and contextual data. In this paper, we present Blue's Data Intelligence Layer (DIL) designed to support multi-source, multi-modal, and data-centric applications. Blue is a compound AI system that orchestrates agents and data for enterprise settings. DIL serves as the data intelligence layer for agentic data processing, to bridge the semantic gap between user intent and available information by unifying structured enterprise data, world knowledge accessible through LLMs, and personal context obtained through interaction. At the core of DIL is a data registry that stores metadata for diverse data sources and modalities to enable both native and natural language queries. DIL treats LLMs, the Web, and the User as source 'databases', each with their own query interface, elevating them to first-class data sources. DIL relies on data planners to transform user queries into executable query plans. These plans are declarative abstractions that unify relational operators with other operators spanning multiple modalities. DIL planners support decomposition of complex requests into subqueries, retrieval from diverse sources, and finally reasoning and integration to produce final results. We demonstrate DIL through two interactive scenarios in which user queries dynamically trigger multi-source retrieval, cross-modal reasoning, and result synthesis, illustrating how compound AI systems can move beyond single database NL2SQL.

</details>


### [193] [How Do LLMs and VLMs Understand Viewpoint Rotation Without Vision? An Interpretability Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15294)
*Zhen Yang,Ping Jian,Zhongbin Guo,Zuming Zhang,Chengzhi Li,Yonghong Deng,Xinyue Zhang,Wenpeng Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文研究了语言智能在空间推理中的作用，提出了视点旋转理解任务，发现LLMs和VLMs在此任务上表现不佳，通过因果干预识别关键注意力头并进行选择性微调来提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注视觉空间智能，但在缺乏视觉信息的情况下，语言智能是否足以赋予模型空间推理能力，以及模型如何处理纯文本输入的空间任务仍未被探索。因此，本文从语言角度研究空间智能中的基本能力：视点旋转理解。

Method: 1. 提出视点旋转理解任务，要求模型根据多步骤的视点旋转和观察文本描述推断最终视点和相应观察；2. 构建相应数据集；3. 通过层间探测分析和头间因果干预揭示模型机制；4. 选择性微调因果干预识别的关键注意力头来提升性能。

Result: 1. LLMs和VLMs在VRU任务上表现不佳，而人类能轻松达到100%准确率；2. 模型在隐藏状态中编码了视点信息，但难以将视点位置与相应观察绑定，导致最终层出现幻觉；3. 选择性微调关键注意力头能提升VRU性能，同时避免通用能力的灾难性遗忘。

Conclusion: 语言智能在空间推理中存在显著局限，当前模型在视点旋转理解任务上表现远不如人类。通过因果干预识别关键注意力头并进行选择性微调是提升模型空间推理能力的有效方法，为理解模型空间推理机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: Over the past year, spatial intelligence has drawn increasing attention. Many prior works study it from the perspective of visual-spatial intelligence, where models have access to visuospatial information from visual inputs. However, in the absence of visual information, whether linguistic intelligence alone is sufficient to endow models with spatial intelligence, and how models perform relevant tasks with text-only inputs still remain unexplored. Therefore, in this paper, we focus on a fundamental and critical capability in spatial intelligence from a linguistic perspective: viewpoint rotation understanding (VRU). Specifically, LLMs and VLMs are asked to infer their final viewpoint and predict the corresponding observation in an environment given textual description of viewpoint rotation and observation over multiple steps. We find that both LLMs and VLMs perform poorly on our proposed dataset while human can easily achieve 100% accuracy, indicating a substantial gap between current model capabilities and the requirements of spatial intelligence. To uncover the underlying mechanisms, we conduct a layer-wise probing analysis and head-wise causal intervention. Our findings reveal that although models encode viewpoint information in the hidden states, they appear to struggle to bind the viewpoint position with corresponding observation, resulting in a hallucination in final layers. Finally, we selectively fine-tune the key attention heads identified by causal intervention to improve VRU performance. Experimental results demonstrate that such selective fine-tuning achieves improved VRU performance while avoiding catastrophic forgetting of generic abilities. Our dataset and code will be released at https://github.com/Young-Zhen/VRU_Interpret .

</details>


### [194] [Diagnosing LLM Judge Reliability: Conformal Prediction Sets and Transitivity Violations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15302)
*Manan Gupta,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个诊断工具包来评估LLM-as-judge框架的实例级可靠性，通过传递性分析和分裂共形预测集揭示了聚合指标掩盖下的广泛不一致性，并识别了不同评估标准的可靠性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM-as-judge框架在自动NLG评估中应用日益广泛，但其在单个实例层面的可靠性仍缺乏深入理解。现有研究主要关注聚合指标，而忽略了每个输入实例的评估一致性，这可能导致对评估系统可靠性的错误认知。

Method: 提出了一个双管齐下的诊断工具包：1）传递性分析，通过检测有向3-循环来揭示被低聚合违规率掩盖的广泛不一致性；2）分裂共形预测集，在1-5李克特量表上提供理论保证的覆盖概率，使用集合宽度作为实例级可靠性指标。该方法应用于SummEval数据集，涵盖四个评估者和四个评估标准。

Result: 研究发现：1）传递性分析显示33-67%的文档至少存在一个有向3-循环，尽管聚合违规率较低（0.8-4.1%）；2）预测集宽度与可靠性显著相关（r_s = +0.576，p < 10^{-100}），且在不同评估者间具有一致性（r̄ = 0.32-0.38）；3）评估标准比评估者更重要，相关性评估最可靠（平均集合大小≈3.0），连贯性中等可靠（≈3.9），而流畅性和一致性评估不可靠（≈4.9）。

Conclusion: LLM-as-judge框架在实例层面存在显著的不一致性，聚合指标可能掩盖了可靠性问题。分裂共形预测集提供了理论保证的实例级可靠性指标，能够有效识别评估困难。评估标准的可靠性差异表明需要针对不同任务优化评估框架，而非仅仅关注评估者选择。

Abstract: LLM-as-judge frameworks are increasingly used for automatic NLG evaluation, yet their per-instance reliability remains poorly understood. We present a two-pronged diagnostic toolkit applied to SummEval: $\textbf{(1)}$ a transitivity analysis that reveals widespread per-input inconsistency masked by low aggregate violation rates ($\barρ = 0.8$-$4.1\%$), with $33$-$67\%$ of documents exhibiting at least one directed 3-cycle; and $\textbf{(2)}$ split conformal prediction sets over 1-5 Likert scores providing theoretically-guaranteed $\geq(1{-}α)$ coverage, with set width serving as a per-instance reliability indicator ($r_s = {+}0.576$, $N{=}1{,}918$, $p < 10^{-100}$, pooled across all judges). Critically, prediction set width shows consistent cross-judge agreement ($\bar{r} = 0.32$-$0.38$), demonstrating it captures document-level difficulty rather than judge-specific noise. Across four judges and four criteria, both diagnostics converge: criterion matters more than judge, with relevance judged most reliably (avg. set size $\approx 3.0$) and coherence moderately so (avg. set size $\approx 3.9$), while fluency and consistency remain unreliable (avg. set size $\approx 4.9$). We release all code, prompts, and cached results.

</details>


### [195] [Generalization in LLM Problem Solving: The Case of the Shortest Path](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15306)
*Yao Tong,Jiayuan Ye,Anastasia Borovykh,Reza Shokri*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文研究了语言模型的系统性泛化能力，通过最短路径规划这一可组合的序列优化问题构建了受控环境，发现模型在空间迁移上表现良好但在长度缩放上因递归不稳定性而失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型是否能系统性泛化仍存在争议，但实证性能受训练数据、训练范式、推理策略等多因素共同影响，导致失败难以解释。需要构建受控环境来分离这些因素并研究系统性泛化能力。

Method: 基于最短路径规划这一经典可组合序列优化问题构建受控合成环境，支持空间迁移（未见地图）和长度缩放（更长视野问题）两个正交的泛化维度。分析学习流程各阶段（数据覆盖、强化学习、推理时缩放）对系统性问题解决的影响。

Result: 模型表现出强大的空间迁移能力，但在长度缩放上持续失败，原因是递归不稳定性。数据覆盖设定了能力上限；强化学习提高了训练稳定性但未扩展这些上限；推理时缩放提升了性能但无法挽救长度缩放失败。

Conclusion: 语言模型在系统性泛化方面存在局限性，特别是在长度缩放维度上。受控环境揭示了不同学习阶段对问题解决能力的影响，为理解模型泛化失败提供了清晰框架。

Abstract: Whether language models can systematically generalize remains actively debated. Yet empirical performance is jointly shaped by multiple factors such as training data, training paradigms, and inference-time strategies, making failures difficult to interpret. We introduce a controlled synthetic environment based on shortest-path planning, a canonical composable sequential optimization problem. The setup enables clean separation of these factors and supports two orthogonal axes of generalization: spatial transfer to unseen maps and length scaling to longer-horizon problems. We find that models exhibit strong spatial transfer but consistently fail under length scaling due to recursive instability. We further analyze how distinct stages of the learning pipeline influence systematic problem-solving: for example, data coverage sets capability limits; reinforcement learning improves training stability but does not expand those limits; and inference-time scaling enhances performance but cannot rescue length-scaling failures.

</details>
